***объезжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объезжать.html>объезжа́ть</a> (18452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объезжать.html>объезжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obʺjezžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объехать.html>объе́хать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объездить.html>объе́здить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to travel <i>(all over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объехать.html>объе́хать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>страну́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obʺjéxatʹ vsju stranú</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">travel all over the country</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:объезжать.html>объезжа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>войска</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obʺjezžátʹ</b> vojska</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">ride around the troops; inspect the troops</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go round, to make a detour, to take the bypass</li>
<li><i>(horses)</i> to break in, to train</li>
<li><i>(a car)</i> to run in</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">необъезженный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neobʺjezžennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объезд.html>объе́зд</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obʺjézd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">объездка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obʺjezdka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объезжать.html>объезжа́ющий</a> (18452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***объектив.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объектив.html>объекти́в</a> (8579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объектив.html>объекти́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obʺjektív</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объектив.html>объекти́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объектив.html>объекти́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объектив.html>объекти́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lens, objective, object glass <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">object focusing or defocusing the light passing through it</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>объ<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ек<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́в</b>

Зализняка).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объехать.html>объе́хать</a> (14438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>to travel <i>(all over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:объехать.html>объе́хать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>страну́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obʺjéxatʹ</b> vsju stranú</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">travel all over the country</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go round, to make a detour, to take the bypass</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>объ<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>е́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,   <a href = vnd.unilang:изолированный.html>изоли́рованное</a> спряжение, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — ^a.     <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́честве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рм</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повелительный.html>повели́тельного</a> накл. <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуются</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:объехать.html>объезжа́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:объехать.html>объезжа́йте</a></i>). <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:объезжать.html>объезжа́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>объ-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ех-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объясниться.html>объясни́ться</a> (10486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объяснить.html>объясни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obʺjasnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объясниться.html>объясни́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obʺjasnítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объясняться.html>объясня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to explain oneself</li>
<li>to be accounted for</li>
<li>to make oneself understood</li>
<li>to have a talk (with), to have it out (with)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объяснить.html>объясни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obʺjasnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объяснять.html>объясня́ть</a> (1356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объяснить.html>объясни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obʺjasnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объяснять.html>объясня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obʺjasnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объяснить.html>объясни́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to explain, to illustrate, to clarify, to illuminate</li>
<li>to account for</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>объ<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:яс.html>яс</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:объяснить.html>объясни́ть</a>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объясняться.html>объясня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obʺjasnjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объясниться.html>объясни́ться</a></b>)

<p><b>объ<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:яс.html>яс</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***объять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:объять.html>объя́ть</a> (16657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:объять.html>объя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obʺjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнимать.html>обнима́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обыма́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come <i>(over)</i>, to envelop, to fill
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:объятый.html>объя́тый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоско́й</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:грусть.html>гру́стью</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obʺjátyj</b> toskój (grústʹju)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">filled with anguish (melancholy)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:объятый.html>объя́тый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пламя.html>пла́менем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obʺjátyj</b> plámenem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">enveloped in flames</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ужас.html>у́жас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:объять.html>объя́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">úžas <b>obʺjál</b> jevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was seized with terror; he was terror-stricken</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to comprehend, to grasp, to embrace
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:объять.html>объя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:необъятный.html>необъя́тное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nelʹzjá <b>obʺjátʹ</b> neobʺjátnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you can't embrace the unembraceable</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
